<review>Anojitos Hector is posted up right in front of the Tustin Parc apartments. They offer tacos, burritos, quesidillas, and tortas. I had asada, pastor, and chorizo tacos. The meat was flavorful and they are priced very reasonably. They have a spicy red salsa and a more m old green. They are both tasty but for anyone who doesn't like spicy while the red isn't too spicy,, imo, it has a little kick. The gentleman who ran thr truck was very nice too. My only thing was the tortillas & meat were a little dry. Will eat again though!</review>< Pics>
